2019. 10. 7. 11:55, (알 수 없음) : 몰라외국인
2019. 10. 7. 11:55, 원준오빠 : 이건 반댕
2019. 10. 7. 11:55, 원준오빠 : 반대로
2019. 10. 7. 11:55, (알 수 없음) : 외국인이 교정해왔는데
2019. 10. 7. 11:55, 원준오빠 : 이건 한편으론
2019. 10. 7. 11:55, (알 수 없음) : Because each mobile device typically stores the data generated by a particular user, each local data distribution does not properly represent the population distribution. This non-IID property definitely hinders the convergence of federated learning and degrades prediction accuracy.  
    On the other hand, this issue may not be critical in traditional distributed machine learning because all training data are accumulated on the central server.
2019. 10. 7. 11:55, (알 수 없음) : 여기선 on the other hand 걍 나뒀는데
2019. 10. 7. 11:55, (알 수 없음) : Because several thousands of devices typically participate in federated learning, the training process is massively distributed, thus causing a huge burden on the backbone (wireless) network. Moreover, the mobile devices are not restricted by their geographic location. 
  On the other hand, in traditional distributed processing, the number of computing servers is not very high, and they are usually located in a single data center.
2019. 10. 7. 11:56, (알 수 없음) : 여기선 on the other hand를 in contrast로 수정하래;;
